;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;Knuckles' Chaotix (JU / 5) Injector File for ROMulan (32x Art)

; 2021-02-XX - GenesisDoes - First Release
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;

;region @Setup
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
; Setup Directives ;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
Define 	ArtPtr32X_Offset 	$02000000
Define	NullLPtr_Terminator $FFFFFFFF
Define	Entry_MasterSH2		$06000000		;Logical ROM offset addr for SH2 (Master)
Define	Offset_MasterSH2	$00077800		;Offset for calculating between raw ROM and SH2 area
MaxSize	$400000				;Maximum Genesis ROM size

;Max size for 32x Art space (art banks) ($20A0000-$222438A)
Define 	Max32xArtSize_Stock $18438A
;Max size for 32x Art space (art banks), including dummy padding ($20A0000-$2227000)
Define 	Max32xArtSize_Full $187000
;EndRegion

;Region @FixedSegs
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
; Fixed Data Segments ;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;

;Region @32xArt
;Region @Ptrs
;!@ Insert ArtPtr32x pts later

;Ptr to APB_Global
StartSeg APB_Global_Ptr	$0077BA4 $0004 Big_Endian
		DWORD	APB_Glbl+ArtPtr32X_Offset
EndSeg

;Ptr to APB_Level
StartSeg APB_Level_Ptr	$0077BD0 $0004 Big_Endian
		DWORD	APB_Level+ArtPtr32X_Offset
EndSeg

;Ptr to APB_SS_Level
StartSeg APB_SS_Level_Ptr	$0077B78 $0004 Big_Endian
		DWORD	(APB_SS_Level-Offset_MasterSH2)+Entry_MasterSH2
EndSeg
;EndRegion

;StartSeg ArtPtr32x Big_Endian $A0000 Max32xArtSize_Stock
;!@ 
StartSeg ArtPtr32x $A0000 Max32xArtSize_Full Big_Endian
